# Nevada water bills — vote roll calls (Pass 2)

Floor Final Passage events: **104**
Committee hearing / work-session events: **287**

Floor votes come from the NELIS Votes tab (full Yea/Nay rolls).
Committee votes come from committee **minutes PDFs** (Nevada usually lists only NO and ABSENT by name; unanimous passes may not list every Yea).
